+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Debug script to understand path resolution"""
+
+import os
+import tempfile
+
+# Create a temporary directory for testing
+with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
+    print(f"Working in temporary directory: {tmpdir}")
+    
+    # Create the exact scenario from the PR description
+    wrappers_dir = os.path.join(tmpdir, "wrappers")
+    os.makedirs(wrappers_dir)
+    
+    # Create /run/wrappers/bin as a symlink that points to a non-empty directory
+    bin_target_dir = os.path.join(tmpdir, "bin_target") 
+    os.makedirs(bin_target_dir)
+    
+    # Put some files in the target directory
+    with open(os.path.join(bin_target_dir, "existing_file"), "w") as f:
+        f.write("content")
+    
+    # Create the symlink /run/wrappers/bin -> /run/wrappers/bin_target
+    bin_symlink = os.path.join(wrappers_dir, "bin")
+    os.symlink(bin_target_dir, bin_symlink, target_is_directory=True)
+    
+    # Create the source directory to move: /run/wrappers/bin-tmp
+    bin_tmp_dir = os.path.join(wrappers_dir, "bin-tmp")
+    os.makedirs(bin_tmp_dir)
+    with open(os.path.join(bin_tmp_dir, "some_file"), "w") as f:
+        f.write("test")
+    
+    print("\n--- Path investigation ---")
+    print(f"bin_symlink: {bin_symlink}")
+    print(f"bin_symlink is symlink: {os.path.islink(bin_symlink)}")
+    print(f"bin_symlink points to: {os.readlink(bin_symlink)}")
+    print(f"bin_symlink resolved: {os.path.realpath(bin_symlink)}")
+    print(f"bin_symlink is_dir: {os.path.isdir(bin_symlink)}")
+    print(f"bin_target_dir: {bin_target_dir}")
+    print(f"bin_target_dir is_dir: {os.path.isdir(bin_target_dir)}")
+    print(f"bin_target_dir contents: {os.listdir(bin_target_dir)}")
+    
+    # Test what path mv would use
+    target_path_for_bin_tmp = os.path.join(bin_symlink, "bin-tmp")
+    print(f"\nTarget path for bin-tmp would be: {target_path_for_bin_tmp}")
+    print(f"Does this path exist? {os.path.exists(target_path_for_bin_tmp)}")
+    
+    # Check if the resolved path is empty
+    resolved_path = os.path.realpath(target_path_for_bin_tmp)
+    print(f"Resolved target path: {resolved_path}")
+    print(f"Does resolved path exist? {os.path.exists(resolved_path)}")
+    
+    # Test what GNU mv actually does
+    import subprocess
+    print("\n--- Testing GNU mv behavior ---")
+    try:
+        result = subprocess.run(["mv", bin_tmp_dir, bin_symlink], capture_output=True, text=True)
+        print(f"GNU mv exit code: {result.returncode}")
+        if result.stderr:
+            print(f"GNU mv stderr: {result.stderr}")
+            
+        print(f"\nAfter mv:")
+        print(f"bin_tmp_dir exists: {os.path.exists(bin_tmp_dir)}")
+        print(f"bin_symlink contents: {os.listdir(bin_symlink)}")
+        if os.path.exists(target_path_for_bin_tmp):
+            print(f"Specific target path exists: {target_path_for_bin_tmp}")
+            print(f"Contents at target: {os.listdir(target_path_for_bin_tmp)}")
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"Error: {e}")

+#!/usr/bin/env python3

+def test_function():

+

+

+        bin_target_dir = os.path.join(tmpdir, "bin_target")
+        os.makedirs(bin_target_dir)
+

+        
+        # Test if rename_with_fallback is being called

+        source = bin_tmp_dir
+        target = bin_symlink
+        
+        # Check what GNU does
+        print("\n--- GNU mv ---")
+        result = subprocess.run(["mv", "-v", source, target], capture_output=True, text=True)
+        print(f"Exit code: {result.returncode}")
+        print(f"Output: {result.stdout}")
+        print(f"Error: {result.stderr}")

+            print(f"Target contents: {contents}")

+            import shutil
+            shutil.rmtree(bin_tmp_dir)

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Final verification test for the mv symlink fix"""
+
+import os
+import tempfile
+import subprocess
+
+def test_mv_symlink_to_directory():
+    """Test the specific case from the PR description"""
+    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
+        print(f"Testing in: {tmpdir}")
+        
+        # Create the exact scenario from the PR
+        wrappers_dir = os.path.join(tmpdir, "wrappers")
+        os.makedirs(wrappers_dir)
+        
+        # Create target directory with files
+        bin_target_dir = os.path.join(tmpdir, "bin_target")
+        os.makedirs(bin_target_dir)
+        with open(os.path.join(bin_target_dir, "existing_file"), "w") as f:
+            f.write("content")
+        
+        # Create symlink
+        bin_symlink = os.path.join(wrappers_dir, "bin")
+        os.symlink(bin_target_dir, bin_symlink, target_is_directory=True)
+        
+        # Create source directory
+        bin_tmp_dir = os.path.join(wrappers_dir, "bin-tmp")
+        os.makedirs(bin_tmp_dir)
+        with open(os.path.join(bin_tmp_dir, "some_file"), "w") as f:
+            f.write("test")
+        
+        print("\n=== Testing GNU mv behavior ===")
+        result = subprocess.run(["mv", bin_tmp_dir, bin_symlink], capture_output=True, text=True)
+        print(f"GNU mv exit code: {result.returncode}")
+        if result.returncode == 0:
+            print("✓ GNU mv succeeded")
+        else:
+            print(f"✗ GNU mv failed: {result.stderr}")
+        
+        # Reset for uutils test
+        import shutil
+        if os.path.exists(bin_tmp_dir):
+            shutil.rmtree(bin_tmp_dir)
+        
+        bin_tmp_dir = os.path.join(wrappers_dir, "bin-tmp")
+        os.makedirs(bin_tmp_dir)
+        with open(os.path.join(bin_tmp_dir, "some_file"), "w") as f:
+            f.write("test")
+        
+        print("\n=== Testing uutils mv behavior ===")
+        uutils_path = "/testbed/target/debug/coreutils"
+        result = subprocess.run([uutils_path, "mv", bin_tmp_dir, bin_symlink], capture_output=True, text=True)
+        print(f"uutils mv exit code: {result.returncode}")
+        print(f"uutils mv stderr: {result.stderr}")
+        
+        if result.returncode == 0:
+            print("✓ uutils mv succeeded")
+            
+            # Verify the result
+            if os.path.exists(bin_symlink):
+                contents = os.listdir(bin_symlink)
+                print(f"Target contents: {contents}")
+                if "bin-tmp" in contents and "existing_file" in contents:
+                    print("✓ Move completed correctly")
+                    return True
+            
+            return False
+        else:
+            print("✗ uutils mv failed")
+            return False
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    success = test_mv_symlink_to_directory()
+    print(f"\n=== Final Result: {'PASS' if success else 'FAIL'} ===")

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Debug script to understand the mv behavior"""
+
+import os
+import tempfile
+import shutil
+import subprocess
+
+# Create a temporary directory for testing
+with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
+    print(f"Working in temporary directory: {tmpdir}")
+    
+    # Create the exact scenario from the PR description
+    wrappers_dir = os.path.join(tmpdir, "wrappers")
+    os.makedirs(wrappers_dir)
+    
+    # Create /run/wrappers/bin as a symlink that points to a non-empty directory
+    bin_target_dir = os.path.join(tmpdir, "bin_target")
+    os.makedirs(bin_target_dir)
+    
+    # Put some files in the target directory
+    with open(os.path.join(bin_target_dir, "existing_file"), "w") as f:
+        f.write("content")
+    
+    # Create the symlink /run/wrappers/bin -> /run/wrappers/bin_target
+    bin_symlink = os.path.join(wrappers_dir, "bin")
+    os.symlink(bin_target_dir, bin_symlink, target_is_directory=True)
+    
+    # Create the source directory to move: /run/wrappers/bin-tmp
+    bin_tmp_dir = os.path.join(wrappers_dir, "bin-tmp")
+    os.makedirs(bin_tmp_dir)
+    with open(os.path.join(bin_tmp_dir, "some_file"), "w") as f:
+        f.write("test")
+    
+    print("\n--- Test 1: mv symlink bin-tmp symlink/bin-tmp (non-overwrite) ---")
+    # First let's check what GNU mv does with -T flag
+    try:
+        result = subprocess.run(["mv", "-T", bin_tmp_dir, bin_symlink], capture_output=True, text=True)
+        print(f"GNU mv -T exit code: {result.returncode}")
+        print(f"GNU mv -T stderr: {result.stderr}")
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"Error: {e}")
+    
+    # Reset
+    if os.path.exists(bin_tmp_dir):
+        shutil.rmtree(bin_tmp_dir)
+    bin_tmp_dir = os.path.join(wrappers_dir, "bin-tmp")
+    os.makedirs(bin_tmp_dir)
+    with open(os.path.join(bin_tmp_dir, "some_file"), "w") as f:
+        f.write("test")
+    
+    # Test without -T flag
+    print("\n--- Test 2: mv bin-tmp bin/bin-tmp (moving into directory) ---")
+    try:
+        result = subprocess.run(["mv", bin_tmp_dir, bin_symlink], capture_output=True, text=True)
+        print(f"GNU mv exit code: {result.returncode}")
+        print(f"GNU mv stderr: {result.stderr}")
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"Error: {e}")
+        
+    print("\n--- Check result ---")
+    if os.path.exists(bin_symlink):
+        try:
+            print(f"bin contents: {os.listdir(bin_symlink)}")
+        except:
+            print("Cannot list bin contents")
+    print(f"bin_tmp_dir exists: {os.path.exists(bin_tmp_dir)}")
+    
+    # Now test with uutils
+    # Reset
+    if os.path.exists(bin_tmp_dir[:-4] if bin_tmp_dir.endswith("-tmp") else None):
+        shutil.rmtree(bin_tmp_dir)
+        
+    bin_tmp_dir = os.path.join(wrappers_dir, "bin-tmp") 
+    os.makedirs(bin_tmp_dir)
+    with open(os.path.join(bin_tmp_dir, "some_file"), "w") as f:
+        f.write("test")
+    
+    print("\n--- Test 3: uutils mv -T bin-tmp symlink ---")
+    try:
+        uutils_mv_path = "/testbed/target/debug/coreutils"
+        result = subprocess.run([uutils_mv_path, "mv", "-T", bin_tmp_dir, bin_symlink], 
+                              capture_output=True, text=True)
+        print(f"uutils mv -T exit code: {result.returncode}")
+        print(f"uutils mv -T stderr: {result.stderr}")
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"Error: {e}")
+        
+    # Reset
+    if os.path.exists(bin_tmp_dir[:-4] if bin_tmp_dir.endswith("-tmp") else None):
+        shutil.rmtree(bin_tmp_dir)
+        
+    bin_tmp_dir = os.path.join(wrappers_dir, "bin-tmp") 
+    os.makedirs(bin_tmp_dir)
+    with open(os.path.join(bin_tmp_dir, "some_file"), "w") as f:
+        f.write("test")
+    
+    print("\n--- Test 4: uutils mv bin-tmp symlink (without -T) ---")
+    try:
+        uutils_mv_path = "/testbed/target/debug/coreutils"
+        result = subprocess.run([uutils_mv_path, "mv", bin_tmp_dir, bin_symlink], 
+                              capture_output=True, text=True)
+        print(f"uutils mv exit code: {result.returncode}")
+        print(f"uutils mv stderr: {result.stderr}")
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"Error: {e}")

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Test script to reproduce the mv symlink issue more accurately"""
+

+import tempfile
+import shutil
+import subprocess
+

+with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
+    print(f"Working in temporary directory: {tmpdir}")
+    
+    # Create the exact scenario from the PR description
+    # /run/wrappers is the target directory
+    wrappers_dir = os.path.join(tmpdir, "wrappers")
+    os.makedirs(wrappers_dir)
+    
+    # Create /run/wrappers/bin (this is the target symlink that points to a directory with files)
+    bin_target_dir = os.path.join(tmpdir, "bin_target")
+    os.makedirs(bin_target_dir)
+    
+    # Put some files in the target directory (this is what makes it "not empty")
+    with open(os.path.join(bin_target_dir, "existing_file"), "w") as f:
+        f.write("content")
+    
+    # Create the symlink /run/wrappers/bin -> /run/wrappers/bin_target
+    bin_symlink = os.path.join(wrappers_dir, "bin")
+    os.symlink(bin_target_dir, bin_symlink, target_is_directory=True)
+    
+    # Create the source directory to move: /run/wrappers/bin-tmp
+    bin_tmp_dir = os.path.join(wrappers_dir, "bin-tmp")
+    os.makedirs(bin_tmp_dir)
+    with open(os.path.join(bin_tmp_dir, "some_file"), "w") as f:
+        f.write("test")
+

+    print(f"bin_symlink is symlink: {os.path.islink(bin_symlink)}")

+    print(f"bin_target_dir contents: {os.listdir(bin_target_dir)}")
+    print(f"bin_tmp_dir contents: {os.listdir(bin_tmp_dir)}")

+    print(f"bin_tmp_dir exists: {os.path.exists(bin_tmp_dir)}")
+    print(f"bin_symlink exists: {os.path.exists(bin_symlink)}")

+        try:
+            print(f"bin_symlink contents: {os.listdir(bin_symlink)}")

+            pass

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Test script to reproduce the mv symlink issue"""
+
+import os
+import tempfile
+import shutil
+import subprocess
+
+# Create a temporary directory for testing
+with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
+    print(f"Working in temporary directory: {tmpdir}")
+    
+    # Create test directories and files
+    source_dir = os.path.join(tmpdir, "source_dir")
+    target_dir = os.path.join(tmpdir, "target_dir") 
+    
+    os.makedirs(source_dir)
+    os.makedirs(target_dir)
+    
+    # Create some files in the source directory
+    with open(os.path.join(source_dir, "file1.txt"), "w") as f:
+        f.write("test content")
+    
+    # Create a directory symbolic link pointing to target_dir
+    symlink_path = os.path.join(tmpdir, "symlink_to_target")
+    os.symlink(target_dir, symlink_path, target_is_directory=True)
+    
+    # Create a temporary directory to move
+    tmp_dir_path = os.path.join(tmpdir, "bin-tmp")
+    os.makedirs(tmp_dir_path)
+    with open(os.path.join(tmp_dir_path, "some_file"), "w") as f:
+        f.write("test")
+    
+    print("\n--- Directory structure before move ---")
+    print(f"source_dir exists: {os.path.exists(source_dir)}")
+    print(f"target_dir exists: {os.path.exists(target_dir)}")
+    print(f"symlink_to_target exists: {os.path.exists(symlink_path)}")
+    print(f"symlink_to_target is symlink: {os.path.islink(symlink_path)}")
+    print(f"symlink_to_target points to: {os.readlink(symlink_path)}")
+    print(f"bin-tmp exists: {os.path.exists(tmp_dir_path)}")
+    print(f"bin-tmp is dir: {os.path.isdir(tmp_dir_path)}")
+    
+    # Test the mv operation that causes the issue
+    print("\n--- Testing mv operation ---")
+    print(f"Attempting: mv {tmp_dir_path} {symlink_path}")
+    
+    # Test with GNU mv first
+    print("\n--- Testing with GNU mv ---")
+    try:
+        result = subprocess.run(["mv", tmp_dir_path, symlink_path], capture_output=True, text=True)
+        print(f"GNU mv exit code: {result.returncode}")
+        if result.stdout:
+            print(f"GNU mv stdout: {result.stdout}")
+        if result.stderr:
+            print(f"GNU mv stderr: {result.stderr}")
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"GNU mv error: {e}")
+    
+    # Clean up and reset for uutils test
+    if os.path.exists(tmp_dir_path):
+        shutil.rmtree(tmp_dir_path)
+    os.makedirs(tmp_dir_path)
+    with open(os.path.join(tmp_dir_path, "some_file"), "w") as f:
+        f.write("test")
+    
+    # Test with uutils mv
+    print("\n--- Testing with uutils mv ---")
+    try:
+        # Build the uutils mv command first
+        build_result = subprocess.run(["cargo", "build", "--bin", "mv"], 
+                                     cwd="/testbed", capture_output=True)
+        if build_result.returncode != 0:
+            print("Build failed!")
+            print(build_result.stdout.decode())
+            print(build_result.stderr.decode())
+        else:
+            uutils_mv_path = "/testbed/target/debug/mv"
+            result = subprocess.run([uutils_mv_path, tmp_dir_path, symlink_path], 
+                                  capture_output=True, text=True)
+            print(f"uutils mv exit code: {result.returncode}")
+            if result.stdout:
+                print(f"uutils mv stdout: {result.stdout}")
+            if result.stderr:
+                print(f"uutils mv stderr: {result.stderr}")
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"uutils mv error: {e}")
+    
+    print("\n--- Directory structure after move ---")
+    print(f"bin-tmp exists: {os.path.exists(tmp_dir_path)}")
+    print(f"symlink_to_target exists: {os.path.exists(symlink_path)}")
+    print(f"symlink_to_target is symlink: {os.path.islink(symlink_path)}")
+    if os.path.exists(symlink_path):
+        try:
+            print(f"Contents of symlink target: {os.listdir(symlink_path)}")
+        except:
+            pass
